- ⚠️ removed the required property `items/teamId` from the response with the `200` status
-  added `#/components/schemas/ItemLinkTypeRecordWithItemLinkTypeRecordEmbed, subschema #2` to the `items/` response property `anyOf` list for the response status `200`

### POST /api/workspaces/global-search
-  added the new optional request property `searchTargets`
-  the request body `application/json` default value changed from `map[archived:false assigneeUserGroupIds:[] assigneeUserIds:[] statusCategories:[] workspaceIds:[]]` to `map[archived:false assigneeUserGroupIds:[] assigneeUserIds:[] searchTargets:[] statusCategories:[] workspaceIds:[]]`
-  the request property `assigneeUserGroupIds` became optional
-  the request property `assigneeUserIds` became optional
-  the request property `statusCategories` became optional
-  the request property `workspaceIds` became optional
-  the `assigneeUserGroupIds` request property default value `[]` was added
-  the `assigneeUserIds` request property default value `[]` was added
-  the `statusCategories` request property default value `[]` was added
-  the `workspaceIds` request property default value `[]` was added
